Growing Unrest Over Land Tax in Jiangdu 89

Villagers Storm County Government Office in Uproar

Over Two Hundred Men and Women Detained

A Yangzhou dispatch: The unrest over land tax inspection in the Second District of this county has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. The police squad of the Public Security Bureau detained fifty men and women the day before yesterday, sending them to the county for interrogation. Later, Cang Liuqi, the head of the Second District, requested the county government to order the villagers to write letters of repentance and release them. County Magistrate Yang replied that he needed to interrogate each person to find out who instigated them before they could be released on bail. This morning (the 22nd), County Magistrate Yang was personally holding court, conducting separate inquiries, when, unexpectedly, the villagers, due to the arrest of many people yesterday, beat drums all night, resulting in thousands of men and women villagers gathering early this morning. Each person held either long incense sticks, bamboo poles, or hoes, and they gathered at Dongguan of Xuningmen and the area facing the Fuyunmen across the river, guarding all the ferry crossings and preventing vegetable and manure carriers from entering the city. Upon hearing the news, the county government immediately telegraphed the police squad of the Public Security Bureau, ordering them to deploy police along the west bank of the canal to establish a tight defense. Around noon, the villagers suddenly seized several small ferries, desperately crossing the river, preparing to enter the city. Seeing the tense situation, the guarding soldiers and police successively closed the Dongguan, Fuyun, Xuning loopholes, and customs gates. Military and police officers went up to the city walls to persuade them, but the villagers' momentum was overwhelming. Finally, they completely gathered outside Fuyunmen, using force to break open the city gate and swarm into the city. At the same time, some people also crossed the wall and entered through Xuningmen. After entering the city, they divided into two routes, heading straight for the county government. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the shops in the city successively closed, and most residents did not dare to go out. Around 2:00 PM, the villagers had gathered at the gate of the county government. The guarding police squad immediately tried their best to stop them. County Magistrate Yang also stood on a wooden stool, intending to give a speech to persuade them, but the voices were too noisy, and the order became increasingly chaotic. In a moment, the villagers smashed the gate of the county government, damaging many of the walls on both sides. They successively rushed into the second gate, and even went to the First Squad of the Police Team to release the villagers arrested yesterday. They swarmed into the main hall of the county government and various offices, the Finance Bureau, the Tax Collection Office, the Police Brigade Headquarters, the Property Protection Association, the Bureau of Weights and Measures, and the county magistrate's residence, destroying everything. They tore up documents and contracts and burned them. When the villagers were about to rush into the county magistrate's residence, County Magistrate Yang escaped through the back door to the office of Central Committee Member Wang, asking for instructions, and notified the Independent Regiment stationed in Yangzhou by telephone, requesting them to send troops to the county government for joint defense. Chen, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and other personnel, who were also in the county government at that time, also exited through the back door. Regiment Commander Lu then immediately sent Deputy Officer Gao with a platoon of soldiers to suppress the situation. Four cavalry soldiers charged in front, clearing the way, allowing them to enter. Therefore, the villagers retreated to the outside of the gate. Subsequently, the Independent Regiment dispatched two more companies of soldiers to rush to the scene, surrounding the villagers from the east and west. The villagers also fled in droves. The army captured many people. The county government immediately notified the guarding soldiers and police at each city gate to close the city gates. The police squad of the Public Security Bureau then conducted separate searches. By 7:00 PM, they had detained about two hundred male and female villagers. All city gates were opened around 8:00 PM. Afterwards, the county government telegraphed reports to the provincial government, the Finance and Civil Affairs Departments, and the Security Office for approval. It was also learned that Wang Yuke, a county government clerk, was beaten by the villagers on the spot and has now been sent to the Bao Kang Hospital for treatment. The damaged items in the county government and the burned files have been photographed for record. (23rd)

Li Yangjing Cables Account of Clash Between Military and Civilians in Chenghai 90

A Shantou dispatch: Some time ago, villagers from Guanshan Township in Chenghai County filed a complaint against the 20th Regiment of the Third Army for rape and robbery. For a time, misunderstandings arose between the military and the civilians, and the situation was quite tense. Later, Li Yangjing, the commander of the Third Army and concurrent Commissioner of Pacification for Eastern Guangdong, strictly investigated and handled the matter, and the situation was resolved. Li Yangjing has telegraphed a detailed report of the case to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee in Nanjing, the Political Affairs Committee of the Southwestern Executive Department in Guangzhou, the provincial government, and the Chaozhou and Shantou associations at home and abroad. The text is as follows: [Regarding the case where the villagers of Guanlong Township in Chenghai County in the jurisdiction killed soldiers of the Chaozhou and Shantou Coastal Security Team and soldiers of Feng Battalion Commander Zhefu of the 20th Regiment, who were ordered to go to the township to investigate and arrest the suspects in this case, and were filed a complaint by villagers Zhang Rennan and representative Yang Min'an, etc. for rape and plunder. I have repeatedly received orders from your committee, your government, and your department to investigate and handle the matter. In addition, I have also received telegrams from overseas Chinese groups inside and outside the country with the same information. I thought that the case was of great importance, and I had to conduct a strict investigation and repeated inquiries, which took a month. It was not until the Jia day of this month that the trial was concluded. Regarding the part of the case where the Security Team seized stolen goods on the river in the township and three team soldiers, including Li Yinfa, were killed by the villagers and three Browning pistols and 300 rounds of ammunition were lost, the testimony of Chen Weinan and Cai Zhanyuan, members of the Chenghai Anti-Japanese Association, and the statements of Zhou Ying, an assistant of the Chenghai Red Cross Branch, Zhang Yuan, the chief of the Shangpeng Public Security Sub-bureau, etc., as well as the various concrete evidence of seizing the corpse, purchasing coffins, burial, and erecting monuments on the same day, is sufficient to prove the facts. However, the local gentry Lu Shouyi, etc., jointly presented a report pushing the blame onto the Anti-Japanese Association, and have repeatedly failed to appear when summoned. Their attempts to cover up and evade investigation are even more obvious. As for the accusation of rape and plunder, the testimony of the so-called raped person, Zeng Xin, contains various contradictions that are too numerous to list. This is sufficient to prove that it is a fabrication. One: Zeng Xin stated that she was robbed of 700 yuan of silver for buying fish and more than ten pieces of clothing, with the clothing carried in ammunition belts and the silver coins held in her hands. However, the testimonies of her husband, Zeng Wanzong, her aunt Zeng Chen, and her husband's brother Zeng Wanqian and his wife all stated that she was carrying a fish stall and there were no such losses. This is sufficient to prove that it is a fabrication. Two: The loss list listed by Zhang Rennan totaled 4,000 to 5,000 yuan. Regarding the paper money, Zhang Rennan stated that it was obtained from Nanyang, but the testimony of his wife Zhang Lu stated that it was the capital recovered from a joint venture that went bankrupt, so the source does not match. Regarding the gold jewelry, Zhang Rennan stated that the gold bracelet lost by his wife was placed under the bed in a wooden box, but the testimony of his wife Zhang Lu stated that it was placed in a small wooden cabinet in the sleeping bed, so the location does not match. According to Zhang Rennan, the four gold rings lost by his daughter-in-law were two that he bought for her, but the testimony of his daughter-in-law Zhang Chen stated that the four gold rings were all bought by her husband one after another, so the origin does not match. This is sufficient to prove that it is a fabrication. Three: Zhang Rennan is an unemployed returned overseas Chinese, with a house as small as a boat and bare walls. Repeated investigations have confirmed that the residents outside the house do not have a main gate. Even if there is such a thing, it would not be so careless as to hide wealth and invite robbery. This is sufficient to prove that it is a fabrication. Four: There are many other discrepancies that have been discussed before and after. Yangjing governs the army with strictness, but I still dare not believe that there was no violation at all. I have sent two officers to investigate secretly, and they have all stated that the accusations are false. I am still afraid that the officers are biased in their protection, so I summoned Xu Richu and Chen Zhi, the detectives sent by the Chenghai County government to guide Feng's troops to the township, to inquire in detail, and they also stated that nothing happened. Moreover, they stated that they did conduct a line-up search for guns when the troops were withdrawn, and they found dozens of copper coins on one soldier, and they were tied up and beaten before being released. All of this is the actual situation of the investigation of all the parties involved in this case. The matter concerns fabrication and attempts to evade responsibility, and while the matter was under strict investigation, the township representatives Yang Min'an and Zhang Rennan, etc., knowing that the false accusation could not be concealed, suddenly sent a telegram explaining on Jing day, which stated that due to the incident of the military coming to investigate the killing and disappearance of the Security Team in the township last month, the villagers misunderstood and fled in droves. The accusations of rape and robbery were made by people from other townships who did not understand the truth. One person spread a rumor, and a hundred people believed it, leading to extreme words and disputes. In fact, when the troops came to the township at that time, they strictly adhered to discipline, etc. At the same time, they jointly presented a report to the office, willing to donate 15,000 yuan for public welfare expenses, requesting lenient treatment and exemption from investigation, and requesting the release of Lin Rongfa and others who were detained and the cancellation of the case. Considering that the villagers were ignorant and incited, and they had already confessed their mistakes, I have approved lenient handling, removed the case, and allocated the donated public welfare expenses to Shantou Sanmin New Village, etc., for subsidies. I will separately submit a report to your committee and department for review and record. (Omitted below)

Party Committee Member Detained for Seducing Young Woman: Dong Zhongxing, a member of the Reorganization Committee of the Yixing County Party Committee, is lustful. On the morning of the 17th of this month, Dong suddenly lured and abducted Yu Shao, the daughter-in-law of Yu of Yixing County, and secretly came to Wuxi by wheel. Unfortunately, his plan was spoiled when Shi Youliang and others from Yixing caught sight of him. Dong knew he could not hide the truth and directly admitted to seducing a married woman. When the wheel arrived at the Wuxi wharf, Shi immediately reported to the Sixth Branch of the local Public Security Bureau, which sent police to detain both the man and woman. After Bureau Member Zhang held a preliminary hearing, he leniently released the Party Committee member, considering his prominent position, and ordered Dong Zhongxing to write a letter of repentance to close the case. Afterwards, the members of the Party Committee in various districts of Yixing and local public figures were greatly angered and filed petitions with the provincial Party Committee, urging a thorough investigation and sending representatives to the province to request the removal of the Reorganization Committee member from his post and severe punishment.

Nantong 94

Construction Department Plans to Build Tongxu Railway: The Construction Department believes that the coastal area of Jiangbei is rich in products, but transportation is inconvenient, making it difficult to export goods. Moreover, the seaports are fragmented, which also has a significant impact on national defense. Therefore, it plans to build the Tongxu Railway, passing through Nantong, Rugao, Taixian, Dongtai, Yancheng, Funing, and Huaiyin, and reaching Xuzhou, as a branch line of the Longhai Railway. It has now appointed engineer Wang Shixi and others to come to Tong to survey the planned route. Military Police Escort on the Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River: Recently, pirates have been appearing frequently in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River. The county magistrates of Tonghaiqi and the chief of the Fourth District of the Water Police, as well as the local military commanders, convened representatives of the Chinese shipping companies operating in the lower reaches of the river in Tong to discuss escort measures. They decided to search and suppress the bandit dens in Hupu with the military police and submit a report to the province to organize an escort team to ensure safety.

Taixian 95

Teacher Punishes Student, Causing Trouble: Zhu, an art teacher at the Local Experimental Primary School, severely beat student Wang Daokuan a few days ago for forgetting to bring his Boy Scout uniform, causing the student to bleed from the nose and faint. The student's parents carried him back home after hearing the news and sought medical attention. According to the doctor, the student's meninges were ruptured, and the injury was serious. It is now heard that the student's parents plan to file a criminal lawsuit with the county government.

Xiaoshan 96

Treacherous Merchants Caught Smuggling Japanese Goods: Since the September 18th Incident last year, all Japanese goods owned by various shops in Xiaoshan have been sealed up by the Anti-Japanese Association and are not allowed to be sold. However, recently, some treacherous merchants have dared to rekindle their activities and sell Japanese goods again. A few days ago, Wang Tianmu and Xie Hengxiang and other shops in Xixing were caught smuggling a large quantity of Japanese goods by the County Anti-Japanese Association. The seized cloth was transferred to the city for review and sealing. At the same time, letters were sent to the supplier shops to impose penalties.

Large Numbers of Refugees Harass Villages: On the afternoon of the 21st, more than one hundred refugees from northern Anhui arrived in the Jiudun area near Guali in the eastern part of Xiaoshan. Among them were men, women, old, and young, with emaciated faces and in a state of extreme distress. Several dozen of the men begged from door to door. If they were refused, they resorted to robbery. Most families with little savings closed their doors. Fortunately, the Guali police station and the local village police collected silver and rice to send them out of the area that night, heading towards Anchang.

Ningbo 97

Bandits Rob Two Stores in Succession: Hengjing in Dongxiang, Yinxian County, is more than ten miles from the city and has more than a thousand households, mostly surnamed Chen. There are more than ten stores in the village, the largest of which are Chen Hengrun Wine Shop and Chen Yongxing Grocery Store. Yesterday (the 21st) around 8:00 PM, five or six bandits suddenly came to the village, each holding a pistol. They first went to Chen Hengrun Wine Shop to search and rob, then went to Chen Yongxing Grocery Store to loot for half an hour before leaving. When the bandits were escaping, Xu Xiaomei, a clerk from Chen Wanxing Rice Shop, and Mo Achuan, a tenant worker from Chen Shun's house, followed them. They were shot by the bandits, causing serious injuries to Xu and Mo.

Shen Xiangmei's Eldest Son Kidnapped: Shen Xiangmei, a resident of Renshou Township in the Sixth District of Yuyao, has long been a salt and salt-pond manager in the five counties of the county and also runs a flower business. He is a wealthy merchant in the county. On the evening of the 18th of this month, around 8:00 PM, during a heavy rain, nine bandits suddenly broke into the house, preventing anyone from making a sound, and conducted a thorough search. Before leaving, they kidnapped Xiangmei's son, Shifan. Fortunately, Shen Xiangmei was doing business in Ningbo that day and was not kidnapped.

(Educational News)

(Important News) 98

Preparations for Chinese Art Exhibition 99

Preparatory Committee Established

Chinese and German Committee Members Appointed

In May of last year, the Ministry of Education approved a letter from the Central Research Institute, which had received a letter from the Chinese Embassy in Germany, stating that since European civilization gradually spread to the East, our ancient Asian civilization has felt that it is behind in everything except for art, in which it can still stand out and compete with Europeans. The Japanese know this and are doing their best to promote Oriental painting and widely promote it in various European countries, pretending to represent Eastern Asian civilization. Recently, the Japanese government has provided 80,000 marks to the Imperial Academy of Art to exhibit the works of more than one hundred modern Japanese painters on a large scale in the Prussian Academy of Art in Berlin. It plans to transport these paintings to various important cities in Germany for exhibition, causing people throughout Germany to spread the word and admire Japanese art. In fact, Japanese painting was originally introduced from our country, and to this day, it still only imitates our country as much as possible. However, our country has never paid attention to publicity, so in the eyes of Europeans, Eastern civilization is only Japan, and not China. Fortunately, there are many people in Germany who study Eastern art and especially appreciate our country's art. Therefore, they automatically opened a Chinese art exhibition two years ago, displaying Chinese ancient paintings, ancient sculptures, ancient bronzes, jade, porcelain, embroidery, etc. for more than a month, which was quite sensational. Unfortunately, the collection was hastily assembled, and the content was not very sufficient, which the Germans deeply regretted. They repeatedly inquired with our embassy, believing that if the Chinese government and the leaders of the educational and art circles could promote and support it, the Germans would be willing to hold another Chinese exhibition to refresh the minds of the new German art world. Therefore, the Chinese Academy of the Buddha in Frankfurt initiated a Chinese art exhibition, which was established with the full assistance of Liu Haisu, the president of the Shanghai School of Fine Arts. It opened on March 19, and a large number of people attended. The number of people who came to view the exhibition every day was endless. However, although Frankfurt is one of the major cities in Germany, it is not as important as the capital. Therefore, President Haisu was invited to visit Berlin. After his arrival, our embassy held a tea party, inviting leaders from the art, political, and academic circles to welcome and discuss the results. German people unanimously hoped that Haisu would hold another large-scale exhibition of modern Chinese paintings in Berlin within two years. On the spot, it was decided that Chinese and German people would jointly organize a preparatory committee. The German side would be led by the German East Asian Art Association, and the Chinese side would be led by the Central Research Institute. The exhibition location would still be the Prussian Academy of Art, and no rent would be charged for the venue. However, the transportation costs of the items, insurance fees, and miscellaneous expenses for the layout of the venue would be covered by the income from the admission tickets. If the income was insufficient, a reserve fund of 30,000 marks would be prepared to make up for the shortfall. The Germans proposed that this fund be borne by the Chinese side. Our embassy believes that this fund can be requested by your academy to the Ministry of Education to be transferred to the National Government for subsidies. The names of the German preparatory committee members are listed above. The Chinese side plans to have your academy president and President Haisu, along with representatives of our embassy, join as preparatory members. Please indicate whether this is appropriate. The Research Institute is very supportive of this matter, but it involves educational administration and has sent a letter to the Ministry of Education to preside over it. The Ministry of Education believes that this overseas publicity is very important for promoting our country's art and should be assisted by the country to achieve its success. It has replied to the Research Institute that this matter should be jointly handled by your academy and this ministry. More than a year has passed, and it has not been handled for two reasons: one is due to financial reasons, and the other is that the time limit for holding the exhibition within two years has not yet become urgent.

In June of this year, the Ministry of Education approved a letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating that Liang Long, the acting charge d'affaires in Germany, stated the same reasons as before. The matter was presented to the 40th meeting of the Executive Yuan and approved. The Minister of Education, the President of the Central Research Institute, the President of the Beiping Research Institute, the Chinese Ambassador to Germany, Chen Shuren, Ye Gongchuo, Liu Haisu, Gao Qifeng, and Xu Beihong have been appointed as members of the exhibition preparatory committee. The committee members held their first meeting in Shanghai on August 6 and decided to establish a preparatory office that day, attached to the International Exchange Office of Publications of the Central Research Institute. Cai Yuanpei, Ye Gongchuo, Chen Shuren, Xu Beihong, and Liu Haisu were elected as standing committee members, with Cai as chairman. The 30,000 mark reserve fund required by the association has been approved by President Wang of the Executive Yuan, who has ordered the Ministry of Railways to allocate the existing funds under Ye's name (more than 40,000 yuan), according to the amount of the reserve fund (30,000 marks) approved by the 42nd meeting of the Executive Yuan, to the preparatory office for its use. The German preparatory committee members are Dr. Salvo, the former German ambassador to China and the president of the East Asian Art Association, Dr. Klumpp, the vice president of the association and a doctor of engineering, Dr. Kmer, a professor at the University of Berlin, Dr. Silber, the chief accountant of the association, Count Haio, the deputy director, Bai Shumen, a professor at the Berlin University of Technology, Dr. Klachow, the director of the National Art Library, the deputy director of publication in charge of the National Museum, and a representative of the German Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Schedules Teacher Certification Examination for Elementary School Teachers Throughout the Province 100

Those Who Have Not Passed the Certification Examination... Will Not Be Allowed to Serve as Teachers

Zhou, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, in view of the lack of teachers in elementary schools in various counties and the fact that teachers have often evaded the certification examinations held in the past, has scheduled the fourth certification examination for April 3rd to 5th of next year. He has specifically issued a public notice to the education bureaus of various counties, ordering all elementary school teachers who have not passed the certification examination to take the examination on time to comply with the regulations. In the future, elementary school teachers who have not passed the certification examination and obtained a permit will not be allowed to be employed. The original order is as follows:

The elementary school teacher examination and certification is an important policy for alleviating the current shortage of teachers and a method for carefully selecting talent and improving education. The department has held it several times and has already provided detailed explanations. It is expected that everyone understands. Now, it is found that there are still many unqualified teachers serving in elementary schools in various counties, and many people who should take the examination and certification have often evaded the examination under various pretexts, which is contrary to the department's intention to carefully select teachers. It is now scheduled that April 3rd to 5th, 22nd year of the Republic, will be the date for the fourth elementary school teacher examination and certification. The registration period is stipulated to be from the date of receiving this order until January 31st, 22nd year of the Republic. The registration fee is originally one yuan and one jiao in consideration of the financial difficulties of elementary school teachers, but it will be reduced by five jiao for this session. All zoning methods and registration review procedures will be handled in accordance with the regulations of the previous certification examination. Once the registration and examination dates for this session are stipulated, they will not be extended. The bureau directors of each county should comply with the stipulated deadlines and order all unqualified elementary school teachers to register for the examination without allowing them to evade it. After this session of certification, all unqualified elementary school teachers will not be allowed to be employed unless they have passed the certification examination. The department aims to rectify teacher fees and will not tolerate any leniency. All elementary school teachers who should take the examination and certification should not wait and see and cause themselves harm. In addition to issuing separate orders, this urgent order is issued to the bureau directors to comply with and handle it, and to inform the public. This is of utmost importance. This order,

Shanghai Boy Scout Grand Review 101

More than 1,100 Boy Scouts Participated

Camped Last Night, Broke Camp at 6 AM This Morning

The Shanghai Council of the Chinese Boy Scouts, to promote the spirit of Boy Scouting, held a city-wide Boy Scout Grand Review ceremony at the Guanghua University campus on Zhongshan Road and Daxilu at 9 AM yesterday. The council had previously sent invitations to various sectors to attend and observe, and also invited Songhu Garrison Commander Dai Ji, 156th Brigade Commander of the 19th Route Army Weng Zhaoyuan, and Mayor Wu Tiecheng to serve as review officers. Yesterday, except for Mayor Wu, who dispatched Huang Wan as his representative due to other engagements, both Dai and Weng personally attended the event. During the opening ceremony, Dai, Weng, and others delivered speeches and addresses. Over a thousand people from various sectors attended to observe. The details are as follows:

Participating Boy Scouts: The Boy Scouts participating in the review included 27 troops from postal workers, commercial workers, Fudan University, Jinan University, Guanghua University, Qingxin School, Liangjiang School, China Women's Physical Education College, Soochow University, Ren'ai School, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the YMCA, Wuyu School, Renyu School, East Asia Physical Education College, Huizhong School, Guangyi School, Guangong School, Xiangong School, Anglo-American School, Hu'an School, and others, totaling more than 1,100 Boy Scouts.

Attendees: Among those who attended the event were Zhu Chongming from the Jiangsu Provincial Boy Scout Council, Gannar from the International Boy Scout Council (transliteration), Zhang Xiang from the Garrison Command, Yu Hongrun from the Public Security Bureau, and Lin Jiyong, Shen Naizhen, Zheng Quan, and others, totaling over a thousand people.

Boy Scout Assembly: The city-wide Boy Scout review ground was located on the campus of Guanghua University. A temporary reviewing stand was set up in the center of the field for the review and opening ceremony. A portrait of Sun Yat-sen was hung in the center of the stand, with the party and national flags crossed on either side. The field was surrounded by bamboo fences. After assembling, the Boy Scout troops were arranged into four columns, led by a military band, followed by the Boy Scout Battlefield Service Corps flag team. The troops were led by commanders Leng Xueqiao and Dai Qijin, entered the field, and paraded around the field before standing in formation.

Review Circumstances: At 10 AM, the Boy Scout band played music, and a flag-raising ceremony was held during the music. The commander-in-chief reported the number of participants to the review officers, and then the parade began. The troops stood in formation around the field, and the review officers, guided by chairmen Wang Gang, Tong Xingbai, Xu Zicheng, and Zhao Weizu, conducted the review. This was followed by a march-past and basic movement drills.

Chairman's Report: After the review, the Boy Scout troops stood at attention in front of the stage to await instructions. Chairman Wang Gang of the presidium began with a report, stating that they felt greatly honored by the presence of Commander Dai, Brigade Commander Weng, the representative of Mayor Wu, and members of all sectors. He said that their only hope was to continue practicing diligently, achieve substantial results, and be able to serve the country. At the same time, he expressed the hope that Commander Dai, Brigade Commander Weng, and others would provide constant guidance to help them improve, which would be greatly appreciated.

Dai Ji's Address: After the chairman's report, Songhu Garrison Commander Dai Ji addressed the audience, saying, "Today, seeing the strong physique and valiant spirit of all you Boy Scouts, I am very impressed. However, you Boy Scouts have attained such physique and spirit through long hours of training, which is no easy task. Therefore, I especially admire the efforts and spirit of the trainers. Our country is now in a critical situation. I hope that the troop leaders will make further efforts to actively train the Boy Scouts, so that they can achieve further success in spirit and physique, and dedicate themselves to the country and fight the enemy in the future. This is my wish."

Weng's Address: Weng Zhaoyuan addressed the audience in a loud voice, saying, "Today, Commander Dai and I came to review you, and we are very grateful for your warm reception. Seeing the excellent performance of your spirit and physique, you are well prepared to save the country. However, the future of saving the country depends on you young people. Without a strong physique and a valiant spirit, it would be difficult to save the country (that is, the future leaders of China will be you young people). Commander Dai just said that he hopes you will continue to work hard in training and prepare to save the country in the future. This is also my sincere hope. In the future, defeating Japan and defeating all imperialists will depend on you young people. I hope you will not forget to save the country and strive forward."

Guest Speakers: Next, Yin Zhiling of the China Aviation Construction Association gave a speech on saving the country through aviation, and Mr. Gannar of the International Boy Scout Council spoke on the topic of Boy Scouts without borders, stating that the sound physique and spirit of Boy Scouts are sufficient to enhance international status. Zhang Shouyong, President of Guanghua University, and others also delivered speeches.

Breaking Camp This Morning: The city-wide Boy Scouts held field exercises at 2 PM yesterday, a campfire at 8 PM last night, and implemented a curfew around the campgrounds starting at 10 PM. After morning exercises at 6:30 AM this morning, they broke camp at 7 AM.

At 7 PM in the evening, a film on the history of the 19th Route Army's battles was screened, moving all the viewers. The West Union Football League: Jinan Shows Early Promise 104

Defeated the Shanghai Westerners Team 3-0

| Created a Three-Game Winning Streak |

Yesterday, the Jinan football team defeated the Shanghai Westerners team 3-0 at the China baseball field. Four to five thousand people watched as Jinan showed early promise and immediately secured victory. The current Westerners team's strength is relatively weak, and their offense and defense both feel weak. In addition, their star player, Sinclair, was injured in the last game against Weidehi and was unable to play yesterday, which further diminished their strength.

Jinan's Shooting Was Slightly Off: Jinan's performance yesterday did not seem to fully utilize their strengths, and their teamwork was not very tight. Fortunately, the defense was safe and sound, with few dangerous moments. The forwards were also somewhat careless, and their shooting was inaccurate, missing many opportunities. The forwards' movements were slightly slow, and they often failed to take advantage of opportunities to break through and score when they reached the opponent's goal. If they can pay attention to this point, the team has great prospects. Yesterday's Westerners team had a very weak forward line, the defense was not solid, and only the goalkeeper was good. Stoker's move to center-back was quite effective.

Luo Haiguang's Excellent Skills: The game started at 3 PM, with Jinan attacking first, putting all their energy into besieging the Westerners' goal from all sides. However, they struggled to find an opportunity. Later, Chen Zhenhe created a scoring opportunity and was about to strike, but his younger brother Zhenxiang was offside, negating the play. Then, Chen Zhenhe stole the ball from the opponent's feet and sent it far forward. Zhenxiang, Haiguang, and Hong Bao tested their scissor formation, passing back and forth, making it difficult for the opponent to track them and waiting for an opportunity. Finally, Luo Haiguang suddenly shot the ball from the right corner of the goal, and it went into the net with a loud sound, which was very beautiful.

Wang Nanzhen's Wonderful Shot: The Westerners' right wing once made a deep solo run, but returned without attacking. Chen Zhenhe led the attack again and saw that the left side was empty, so he sent the ball far over. New left-wing general Wang Nanzhen returned it to the front of the goal, and Chen Zhenxiang safely got the ball in an unguarded spot. However, he was too hasty and missed the shot, resulting in a wild pitch. Jinan's aggressive offensive meant that there were many scoring opportunities. Luo Haiguang had three chances but failed to take advantage of them. Three fierce shots went over the goal, which was a great pity. Chen Zhenhe accurately spotted Mei Hongshi and sent out a corner kick, which was headed towards the goal, but was caught again. Jinan repeatedly missed opportunities, which was regrettable, but the team was spirited and fought hard. Chen Zhenhe orchestrated well, Luo Haiguang shuttled from the middle, and Wang Nanzhen shot powerfully at the goal, the ball flying swiftly into the net. This goal was a successful example of the forwards' teamwork, and the excellent shot made it even more impressive. Jinan led 2-0 at halftime.

Mo Tan Got His Wish: "Little Black Coal" Chen Zhenhe orchestrated the entire team and worked hard, but he often failed to command as he wished and could not fulfill his ambitions. In the 20th minute of the second half, Mo Tan struggled to fight the enemy, broke through three barriers, and went deep into the enemy's camp. He received a pass from Luo Haiguang and succeeded, making the score 3-0. Afterwards, Haiguang and others attacked fiercely again, and Black Coal shot another goal, but failed to score. Mei Hongbao repeatedly joked with the enemy and made few contributions. The situation in the second half was uneventful.

Yesterday, the Youyou football team drew 2-2 with the strong British Weidexia team at Yiyuan. However, this was the result of the first half. In the second half, Youyou completely collapsed and conceded seven consecutive goals, resulting in a 9-2 defeat. This was a game from the West Union First Division League. There were few spectators, mostly foreign soldiers with blond hair and blue eyes.

The area was empty, and Sun Huipei shot it in, making the score 2-2 at halftime.

Finally, they conceded three more goals: (1) Beggle, (2) Palmero, (3) Beggle, ending the game 9-2.

Hui and Ka Defeat the Two Luos: This morning, the fifth set, which had not been decided, continued, and Hui and Ka took a 5-1 lead and won 6-3. The Shanghai team then won two points.

Lin Baohua Defeats Lun Qiang: After Lin Baohua defeated Lun Qiang, the Shanghai team won three matches to zero against Hong Kong. The final two matches were irrelevant to the outcome. Lin played the first set against Lun in the morning and finished it in the afternoon with scores of 6-3, 6-2, and 6-2. This was very impressive. Lun Qiang was slightly diminished, while Lin was exceptionally good. His serves were powerful and he completely defeated Lun Qiang. Xu Huipei Defeats Hui Te: Xu is an 18-year-old rising star from Hong Kong. His speed and accuracy made it impossible for Hui Te to run. The Two Luns Defeat Lin and Zheng: Shanghai took a 5-2 lead in the first set, but lost the set due to Zheng's repeated double faults and net touches. Shanghai was still diminished in the second set, and Zheng's double faults were still frequent. Although Lin's serve was good, the two Luns won with perfect cooperation. Shanghai took a 4-1 lead in the third set, but due to Zheng's weakness, the ball often went out of bounds and touched the net. The two Luns were very steady and deserved to win.

In total, Shanghai won three matches and Hong Kong won two.

New Basketball Techniques (18) (Do Not Reprint) Original Author: Claire Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin 112

Dr. Walter E. Meanwell, basketball coach at the University of Wisconsin, teaches his team to focus on fast attacks, quick passes, agile turns, and blocking opponents. The diagram shows one of Dr. Meanwell's techniques for throwing the ball in from the sidelines during an attack.

Player #1 stands outside the sideline in the opponent's zone and throws the ball in. Player #2 takes a few steps forward, tricking their defender into thinking they will receive the ball and shoot. Then, they run to near Player #3 and stop. At this time, Player #3's defender will be blocked by Player #2. Player #3 can rush forward to the space left by Player #2 and receive the ball from Player #1. Player #1 passes the ball to Player #3, who turns and dribbles the ball into an open space, shooting from 10 feet away from the basket. Otherwise, they can pass the ball to Player #4 or #5, who are running towards the basket.

Local News

Chairman Lin's Arrival in Shanghai from Fujian Yesterday Afternoon 113

A Short Stay of Three or Four Days Before Returning to Nanjing

Lin Sen, Chairman of the National Government, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at approximately 6:00 AM aboard the China Navigation Company's ship "Zhenyijianala" from Xiamen, accompanied by his aides Lin Zhitang and Ben Ding. However, due to fog, the ship was delayed and only arrived at around 11:00 AM, docking at the Pootung (Pudong) Blue Funnel Wharf. The Shanghai Municipal Police Commissioner, Wen Hong'en, and Fujian Provincial Government Committee member Jiang Pingfan, along with others, went to the wharf to welcome him. In addition to dispatching an armed police squad to protect the wharf, the Third District Police Bureau of Pootung, the Shanghai Municipal Government also sent Captain Zhang Zhensheng leading a military band to the wharf to welcome him. After disembarking, Chairman Lin transferred to a police launch and crossed the river to the Jianghai Customs Wharf, then quickly returned to his private residence on Rue du Père Robert (Jin Shenfu Road) to rest. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Land Bureau Director Jin Liren, and Lin's relatives and friends, including Lin Wojiang, visited him one after another. At 4:00 PM, Lin went out to visit friends. A reporter from the Central News Agency went to Lin's residence yesterday afternoon to present his card and pay his respects, inquiring about the recent situation in Fujian Province. According to Lin, he had been away from Fujian for a long time, and this return visit made him feel that the municipal administration of Fujian Province had made progress compared to before, and that Xiamen had progressed even faster. As for the rumors that the Fujian Provincial Government would be reorganized, he said he was not aware of it. The Central Government would naturally rectify any dysfunctional organizations. As for the 19th Route Army's entry into Fujian to suppress bandits, they had achieved repeated successes, and the front line had already advanced to the Longyan area. The remaining bandits would soon be wiped out. Chen Guohui was still in custody and would be tried by a military tribunal, which was planned to be jointly established by the Fujian Provincial Government, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and the courts. Lin said that he had already submitted his opinions on the investigation team's report to the Foreign Affairs Committee for discussion, because it concerned foreign affairs, and it was currently inconvenient to make it public. Lin plans to stay in Shanghai for a short time, and will return to Nanjing in three or four days.

Zhang Boling Discusses the Situation in Shandong 114

Liu's Occupation of Jiaodong Interferes with Civil Administration

Han's Rash Initiation of Warfare is Also Unforgivable

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, Zhang Boling, the president of Nankai University, came to Shanghai from Nanjing the day before yesterday to report to the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance on the process of mediating the war between Han Fuqu and Liu Zhennian in Shandong. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Zhang at the Xinhuizhong Inn yesterday to inquire about the situation and future of the Shandong war. Zhang replied as follows:

Occupying Jiaodong: Although Liu Zhennian's troops are called a division, they are actually tens of thousands of soldiers. For several years, they have occupied twelve counties in Jiaodong, appointing and removing local officials, and their military expenses are obtained locally. After Han Fuqu took charge of the provincial administration, he tried his best to unify the administration of the entire province. Although local officials in Jiaodong were gradually appointed by the provincial government, Liu's monthly military expenses were determined by Minister He of the Ministry of Military Administration to be 170,000 yuan, with 100,000 yuan allocated by the Central Government each month and 70,000 yuan subsidized by Shandong Province. Later, the Shandong Provincial Government agreed to increase the subsidy to 100,000 yuan, but Liu Zhennian insisted that Shandong Province must subsidize 150,000 yuan. After several consultations, it was only agreed to reduce it to 145,000 yuan, otherwise it would still be obtained from the defense area. Thus, the war started.

Concentrated in Three Counties: Liu Zhennian's troops were prepared for the war early, and stored grain in the three counties of Yexian, Laiyang, and Jimo, and built defense works. Therefore, as soon as the war started, Liu's troops abandoned other places and retreated to the three counties, and Han's troops took a siege formation. When I (Zhang refers to himself below) arrived in Jinan, Han Fuqu was already in Weixian, and I immediately sent a telegram to inform him that I would go to meet him. The next day, Jiang Bocheng returned from Weixian and said that it was not necessary to go, and Han would return to Jinan soon. So I waited in Jinan for Han to return. When we met, I advised him that in this critical period of national crisis, civil war should not be initiated under any circumstances, so as not to give enemy countries an excuse. Han also deeply agreed, but he could not bear to let the people of Jiaodong be ravaged by Liu, since he was in charge of the provincial administration. Then the Central Government sent Commissioners Fan and Li to Shandong to investigate, but in reality, it had already entered a stalemate. I then left Shandong.

Key to the Solution: To be fair, Han Fuqu's achievements in governing Shandong and his military discipline are commendable, and cannot be compared with what Liu Zhennian did in Jiaodong. However, he launched the war without asking for instructions from the Central Government, which is also unforgivable. Now Han Fuqu firmly insists that Liu's troops leave Shandong Province. In principle, since Liu's troops are part of the national army, the Central Government has the right to decide where Liu is stationed, and local officials should not be allowed to have any preferences. The key to the problem should be that the troops should not interfere in civil administration, which is the proper way. The solution in the future should also be that Liu's troops should reduce their defense area and not interfere in civil administration.

Returning North Tomorrow: Zhang came south this time to attend the physical education conference convened by the Ministry of Education (which closed on the 20th). He stayed in Shanghai for four days. In addition to attending the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance and the Physical Education Promotion Association meetings, he was invited to give speeches at Shanghai Middle School (the day before yesterday), Wuben Girls' High School (today), and the anniversary of the founding of the school. The Nankai University Alumni Association held a banquet at the YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge yesterday afternoon. He was very busy with socializing and giving speeches. He will return north tomorrow afternoon.

Tibetan Lamas Telegraph Request for Troop Deployment to Defend Against Tibet 115

A reporter from the Shen Shi Telegraph Agency met yesterday with Jie Shengjun, the representative of the Sichuan Provincial Government, who showed him a recent telegram from various Tibetan Buddhist monasteries in Xikang, hoping to cease hostilities and defend against foreign aggression. The telegram is recorded below (titles omitted):

We lamas have grown up in the borderlands and are unable to receive the same protection as the people in the interior. Since the founding of the Republic of China, Tibetan troops have invaded, and under the force of violence, we have suffered all kinds of abuses. By the seventh year of the Republic, Tibetan troops had occupied the hinterland of Xikang, leaving only thirteen counties in the area of Pida River. Alas, we Kang people have since felt the extreme bitterness of being in deep water and scorching fire. People have ear taxes, animals have hoof taxes, food is plundered, and women are subjected to their lewd abuse. The extent of the cruelty is too much to describe. In June of the nineteenth year, monks from Dajie Monastery colluded with Tibetan troops and started a conflict, which has dragged on for two years, and Ganzhan has fallen. The people of Xikang have been looking forward day and night to the Central Government's furious anger and strictly ordering Commander-in-Chief Liu to lead his troops out of the pass to launch a large-scale punitive expedition. However, because the Tibetan situation is treacherous, they have secretly purchased and transported foreign weapons and actively increased their troops, while on the surface they are still loyal to the Central Government and conducting reconciliation. This has been ambiguous and suspended until now. Fortunately, the Central Government has seen through their treachery and ordered Commander-in-Chief Liu in March of this year to be responsible for handling the affairs of Xikang. He then mustered his troops and launched an attack on schedule. The Tibetans again took the initiative, intending to gain an inch after another. Relying on the commander's leadership and the soldiers' dedication, they recovered Ganzhan in one battle, and Deg, Dengke, and Baiyu counties in the next. There are no more traces of Tibetan troops on the east bank of the Jinsha River. We hope that we can continue our efforts to pacify the whole of Xikang, so that the people in various places who are groaning under the iron hooves of the Tibetan bandits can all enjoy peace and security, avenge their long-standing grievances, and promote national prestige. According to what the lamas have seen and heard, the garrison on the east bank of the Jinsha River has been prepared and should be able to advance in one go and recover all the lost land. However, it has been delayed for a long time and is still silent. After suspicion and questioning, we have investigated everywhere and learned that a war is about to break out in eastern Sichuan. The officers and soldiers on the front line are deeply afraid of being implicated and cut off from support, and cannot help but hesitate and delay. The lamas initially did not believe it, thinking it must be just rumors. After detailed investigation, it seems to be true. However, we still believe that in this critical period of national crisis, when the people of the country are advocating the abolition of civil war, no ambitious military man would dare to risk such a great injustice. Moreover, Supervising Commissioner Liu, who is stationed in eastern Sichuan, is about to send troops to Hubei Province to help the country in its emergency. How could he be manipulated by others to engage in fratricide and allow one or two trouble-makers to stir up internal strife? Judging from reason and principle, this cannot be true. However, according to the reliable news recently transmitted from the stove merchants, the situation in eastern Sichuan has taken a sharp turn for the worse. If we do not quickly seek to eliminate it, it will inevitably hinder the overall plan and affect the situation in Xikang. The efforts of half a year of bloody battles will be in vain. Thinking of the future, we are extremely worried. Considering that Commander-in-Chief Liu has taken on this difficult task of using troops against Tibet with the strength of one region, and has not hesitated to make great sacrifices to drive the Tibetan troops to the west bank of the Jinsha River in a short period of time, the Central Government should be concerned about the defense of the western border and give him sufficient material assistance and superior spiritual support, so that he can concentrate on achieving complete success and permanently secure the situation in Xikang. Unexpectedly, things have not gone as hoped and obstacles have arisen, and the crisis is imminent. The lamas are as close to the Han people as to heaven and hate the Tibetans as enemies. The pain is deeply felt and it is difficult to remain silent. As a last resort, we can only telegraph to you, the gentlemen of the central government, ordering Supervising Commissioner Liu of Chongqing to immediately cancel war preparations and stop military actions, so as not to endanger national defense and make it impossible to clean up. At the same time, Commander-in-Chief Liu is still responsible for concentrating his forces and focusing on Tibet. We also hope that our military and political authorities and organizations in the capital and abroad will unanimously advocate and jointly stop the outbreak of the Sichuan War in order to consolidate national defense. The telegram is of the utmost urgency and imploring. Signed by the lamas of Ding'an Que Monastery, Nanwu Monastery, Zhuwo Monastery in Luhuo, Shou'ning Monastery, Huiyuan Monastery in Daofu, Donggu Monastery in Garze, Jiazi Monastery in Zhanhua, Alu Monastery in Dege, Gatuo Monastery in Baiyu, and Dingning Monastery in Ba'an.

Cai Yuanpei and Others Rescue Chen Duxiu 116

Yesterday, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Xingfo, Liu Yazi, Lin Yutang, and other leaders of Shanghai's academic circles sent a telegram to the Central Committee of the Kuomintang and the National Government in Nanjing. The text is as follows:

To the Central Committee of the Kuomintang and the National Government in Nanjing: We have heard that Chen Duxiu was arrested and sent to Nanjing while he was ill, and we are very concerned. This man promoted revolution in his early years and co-founded the "Guomin Ribao" in Shanghai with Zhang Puquan and Zhang Xingyan. After the Restoration, he assisted Bai Liewu in governing Anhui and made contributions. During the May Fourth Movement, he advocated new culture and indirectly helped the National Revolution. These contributions should not be erased by personal grudges. Unfortunately, due to differences in political views, he went astray. However, because he opposed the policy of violence and condemned the Red Army as bandits, he was expelled from the Communist Party. He is actually no different from the Communist Party members in the parliaments of various constitutional countries in Europe and America. We hope that you will show compassion for the old and cherish talent, and give him a chance to reform himself. It would be a great blessing for academia and culture. We await your orders with trepidation.

Repurpose Condolence Banners by Dyeing: Gu Xiyuan of the Zhenxing Wool Spinning Factory, a member of the Shanghai Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army Support Association, suggested to the association yesterday: "Dear Sirs, autumn is high in the borderlands, and severe winter is approaching. The isolated army in the wilderness lacks clothing and equipment. I suggest that we make use of the condolence banners and other cloth items discarded at funerals by various sectors (such as the more than ten thousand pairs of condolence banners from the memorial service for the former 19th Route Army), dye them, and then collect artificial cotton and other materials. Tens of thousands of winter clothes can be made quickly. This would be of great benefit to the Northeast Volunteer Army. If my humble suggestion is adopted, I am willing to contribute my efforts to the dyeing. Please make a public decision and implement it."

Various Groups Welcomed He Minhun Yesterday 124

Telegraph from Li Liejun and Others Requesting Troop Deployment to Recover Lost Territories 125

Li Liejun and others telegraphed, stating: "The Japanese militarists have forcibly occupied the three northeastern provinces for years. At the beginning of the incident, the authorities adopted a policy of non-resistance and begged for pity from the empty and powerless League of Nations. The League of Nations repeatedly held meetings and debated, and finally dispatched an investigation team. The team's report was signed in Beijing on September 4 this year, a full year since the Shenyang Incident. During this time, we have not heard of the government sending a single soldier out of the pass to recover lost territories. They only knew how to rely on the League of Nations, waiting for rescue from the bottom of a well. Now, the report has been repeatedly twisted and turned before being released to the world. After reading it, we cannot help but sigh at the authorities' misjudgment in relying on the League of Nations for years. To briefly discuss its content, the major purpose of this investigation team's visit to the East was to investigate the truth of the Sino-Japanese dispute. In terms of facts, the investigation team knew that the Shenyang Incident was due to a carefully prepared plan by Japan, implemented with swift and precise methods, and could not be regarded as a legitimate means of self-defense. It also knew that the establishment of the puppet organization in Manchuria was created by the Japanese military authorities, not by the free will of the local people. Japan clearly harmed China's sovereignty, independence, and territorial and administrative integrity through unilateral military action. Its violation of the League of Nations Covenant, the Nine-Power Treaty, and the Kellogg-Briand Pact cannot be justified no matter how hard they try. To maintain the dignity of the above treaties, the investigation team should have suggested that the League of Nations advocate restoring the original state before the September 18 Incident last year and impose effective sanctions on Japan in accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant. Instead, it suggests that a special system of government be organized in our three northeastern provinces under an advisory council, with a special police force trained by foreigners to maintain internal security. Other tax collection agencies in the three northeastern provinces should be supervised by foreigners, and the chief advisor of the central bank should be a foreigner. Our government has no right to interfere with the appointment of the so-called administrative head of the autonomous government and must hire foreign advisors with a significant proportion of Japanese. Furthermore, the prohibition of our troops from being stationed and the prohibition of boycotting Japanese goods in the treaty all contradict international treaties. If the League of Nations adopts its recommendations in the future, it will not only go against the wishes of our people but also expose its own weaknesses. The misjudgment of relying on the League of Nations has been proven. It is imperative to dispatch a large number of troops out of the pass to actively resist the Japanese army in conjunction with the volunteer army originally in the three northeastern provinces, recover lost territories, and shift the focus of various countries. Only then can there be justice in the world. We hope that our countrymen will recognize the impending catastrophe, mourn the imminent national demise, and act swiftly and unanimously. Those who openly advocate resistance but secretly plot to contain it are cutting themselves off from the people of the country, and this association vows to abandon them together with the people of the country. We telegraph this with anger and look forward to clear instructions. Li Liejun, Zhang Dingfan, Sun Jiaya, Xu Suzhong, and Xu Yuanfu, standing directors of the Jiangxi Public Association, bow their heads."

National Loan Exhibition 129

Closing Ceremony Held This Morning

Total Expenses During the Two Weeks: More Than 7,000 Yuan

Daily Number of Visitors: Over 30,000

The National Loan Exhibition in this city, which began on Double Tenth Day, concluded yesterday after two weeks of exhibition. The closing ceremony was held this morning, and the conclusion was processed. Details are recorded as follows:

Yesterday's Conclusion: A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency specially visited Cao Zhendong, Director of the National Loan Exhibition Hall, yesterday. According to him, although various manufacturers have requested an extension of the exhibition period, it was decided to close on time due to financial difficulties. The conclusion has been processed, and business and displays ceased at 10 PM on the 23rd. The closing ceremony was scheduled for 10 AM on the 24th. The exhibition this year lasted two weeks and cost approximately 7,000 yuan. A total of 98 manufacturers participated, with an average daily business income of over 30,000 yuan. Over 10,000 pieces of national loans were displayed. The daily number of visitors was very crowded, averaging over 30,000 from 8 AM to 10 PM.

Closing Ceremony: The National Loan Exhibition notified various manufacturers yesterday, stating: "To Whom It May Concern, the Association has decided that the temporary market will cease business on the 23rd of this month, and the closing ceremony will be held at 10 AM on the 24th. Director Wu of the Social Affairs Bureau will attend the ceremony to preside over it. In addition to sending separate letters, we hope that the manager or representative of your company will attend to show solemnity." The order of the closing ceremony is as follows: (1) All stand at attention, (2) Sing the Party song, (3) Pay the highest respects to the Party and national flag and the portrait of the Founding Father, (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Founding Father's will, (5) Silence, (6) The chairman delivers the closing speech, (7) Guests deliver speeches, (8) Closing.

Zhu Tingqi Inspects Salt Affairs in Changlu 133

Commissioner of the Salt Affairs Inspection Office and Director of the Salt Affairs Administration Zhu Tingqi, after inspecting Erhuai, Zhejiang, and Shandong, learned that since the reorganization of each district, the affiliated staff have been honest, self-disciplined, and diligently serving the public. Therefore, tax revenue has been increasing daily, which is greatly appreciated. He has now come to Tianjin with General Inspector Zeng Yangfeng and will travel to Hangu, Tanggu, and other places to investigate the salt affairs situation. It is reported that the inspection revealed that the salt pans in the Lu district were the earliest built and the most complete in scale, serving as a model. However, due to the many national crises in recent years, management has been difficult. The suppression of private salt has not been rectified, and private beaches and private saltpeter are rampant. Although tax revenue has not been reduced, sales have actually decreased. He has personally instructed the Changlu salt transport officer and the inspection sub-office's managing director to cooperate and actively rectify the situation, so that private beaches can be eliminated in the future. As for private saltpeter, it requires the assistance of local officials. It is planned that when he returns to Beijing after inspecting each district, he will draft a plan and request the Minister of Finance to consult with the local officials of Hebei and Henan to order them to cooperate in the crackdown.

Grain and Oilseed Industry 134

Appeals for Reduction of Northeast Soybean Tax

The Shanghai Grain and Oilseed Industry Association submitted a petition to President Song Dai of the Nanjing Executive Yuan and Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "We believe that the soybeans produced in the Eastern Provinces are extremely abundant. The annual exports are substantial, and the daily needs of the people in the mainland depend on them. Historically, imports and exports have only been taxed at half the rate, which is to benefit the people. Since the abolition of the Likin tax, oil from the Eastern Provinces has been subject to an export tax of 4.5 yuan per 100 catties, and soybeans 0.9 yuan. Since the September 18 Incident last year, the violent Japanese have seized the Northeast Customs under the guise of the puppet state of [Manchukuo]. Our government does not want to take retaliatory action to avoid causing suffering to the local and mainland people, so it has not changed the usual transportation practices for its products. Now, the puppet state controlled by the violent Japanese has begun to levy import taxes on all goods traded with China. Therefore, our government had no choice but to implement a policy of closing the Northeast Customs and promulgated a method of levying taxes in other places on September 24. According to the regulations for national loans and factory-made goods, soybeans are still taxed at the usual rate. However, since the goods are exported from the place of origin, they are taxed first, and when they arrive, they are taxed again. The double taxation in different places has doubled the burden, which merchants can hardly bear in these difficult times. However, in order for the government to implement the sales ban policy, they reluctantly accept it and have nothing to say. However, it is found that the previous method lists the goods from Dalian as foreign goods, with a tax of 1.25% of the value of oil at any time, and 10% of the value of soybeans, plus the collection of supplementary relief and wharf donations and dredging donations, all as before. Taxed in this way, the rate has increased several times compared to before. While our members were still shocked, the Ministry of Finance secretly ordered the customs on the 12th of this month to suddenly change the predetermined method. All oils exported from Yingkou and Andong are also listed as foreign goods, and the tax rate is set in the same way as the goods from Dalian. The customs immediately received the order to collect the tax on the 14th. We have found that soybeans have always been taxed as domestic goods. The old tax law set the oil rate at 4.5 yuan, plus the collection of surcharges, so each basket of 350 catties paid about 1.5 yuan in tax. Now, it is listed as foreign goods, with a tax of 1.25% of the value. Based on an estimated value of 10 yuan, the tax payable is 1.2 yuan, plus the surcharges and export taxes, totaling more than 5 yuan per basket in customs silver, which is about 7 yuan in Shanghai silver. Compared to the past, it has increased by more than three times. Soybeans exported from Dalian are also taxed as foreign goods, with a tax of 10% of the value. Based on an estimated value of 3 yuan, the tax payable is 3 yuan, plus the surcharges and export taxes, totaling about 0.4 yuan in customs silver per 100 catties. Compared to the past, it has also increased by more than three times. Moreover, the change in oil taxation was not widely publicized in advance, and the order was sudden, making it impossible for merchants to plan ahead for goods already in transit, which further increased losses. This is no different from putting those who deal in soybeans in a situation of utter extinction. We believe that apart from dealing in miscellaneous grains, rice, and wheat, our members rely solely on soybeans. After the Shanghai War this year, finances are tight, and turnover is extremely difficult. In addition, the sharp drop in the market price of rice and wheat has resulted in even greater losses. Now, with the added burden of soybean taxation, the entire miscellaneous grain industry will inevitably be fundamentally shaken. If it is unfortunately impossible to maintain and continue, then the domestic sales of grain produced in the Northeast will be cut off, which will make the people in dire straits feel even more difficulty in making a living. Thinking of this, we cannot bear it. Moreover, soybean oil is a necessary seasoning, and soybeans are a staple food for the poor. Both are indispensable to daily life, but domestic production and demand are vastly different. The people rely solely on the Eastern Provinces. Now, if such a large tax rate is suddenly added, the merchants are directly affected, and the general poor who need daily necessities are indirectly burdened. At a time when agriculture and commerce are declining and people's livelihoods are deteriorating, how can our people bear it? In short, this time the government had no choice but to implement the policy of sealing off the Northeast Customs and levying taxes in other places. If it is still levied at the usual tax rate, then the people are subject to the double tax from both import and export, and based on the patriotic conscience, who would not want to reluctantly accept it? However, if it is levied excessively and taken without satiation, causing the people to suffer this unbearable pain in addition to double taxation, then forbearance is tantamount to announcing their own death sentence. We earnestly list the situation below and appeal to the esteemed director to grant a review and approval to classify soybeans exported from Andong and Yingkou uniformly as national loans and to levy taxes in other places at the usual tax rate. Although Dalian belongs to a Japanese concession, in order to be considerate of the difficulties of merchants and to consider the livelihood of the people, we also request that the handling of soybeans exported from there be approved in the same way to avoid shaking the entire grain merchant. In the telegraph, we are filled with apprehension and await your orders. Shanghai Grain and Oilseed Industry Association, Chairman of the Committee Gu Xinyi bows his head."

Representative of the Luoyang Dazhonghua Daily 137

Yesterday's Reception for Local Journalists

Report on the Closure by the County Party Department

Request to Uphold Justice and Provide Assistance

The Luoyang Dazhonghua Daily, founded by Jia Xingyuan and others, was sealed by Xie Qing, a member of the County Party Department, and Tang Mingzhi, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, along with the security team and police team on the fifth of this month. The newspaper's president, Jia Xingyuan, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday, and at 6 p.m. yesterday, he hosted local journalists at the Nanjing Hotel on Nanjing Road. More than ten reporters from various newspapers attended. During the meeting, the chairman reported on the closure of the newspaper and requested that justice be upheld and assistance provided, and that telegrams be sent to the Henan Provincial Party Department, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and the Provincial Government, to handle the matter impartially and order the lifting of the seal. The declaration of the newspaper is transcribed below: "Considering that during the brutal Japanese invasion, the capital was moved and Luoyang became the central hub of the Party and the State, the local area gradually prospered. In order to promote open-mindedness and public opinion, we specially founded the Dazhonghua Daily with a few like-minded comrades. Since its publication, it has been praised by society and has developed considerably. Just as we were planning to gradually expand, on the fifth of this month, Xie Qing, a member of the County Party Department, and Tang Mingzhi, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, led fifty or sixty members of the security brigade and police team, fully armed, as if facing a formidable enemy, surrounded the newspaper office, and looted everything. They also fabricated instructions to arrest the president and vice president. Xingyuan, fortunately, received information ten minutes in advance and managed to escape. Xie Qing and others fabricated evidence and falsely reported 'reactionary' activities after the fact. Such destruction of public opinion and oppression of the people not only violates the central government's repeated public announcements guaranteeing the people's freedom of assembly, association, speech, publication, and residence, but also disregards the law, acts arbitrarily, and not only has our newspaper suffered, but this sets a terrible precedent, which is a major crisis for the future of our press. Therefore, we have specially come to Shanghai to report the incident, and humbly request the gentlemen of the press to provide assistance so that we can punish these villains and resume publication. We are extremely anxious. We respectfully submit the actual reasons for the closure and the clear evidence that there is no reactionary activity, as listed below for your scrutiny."

Actual Reasons for the Closure: (1) Luoyang has another newspaper, the Heluo Daily, which is subsidized by the Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government. Because Xie Qing is in charge, he has repeatedly requested a merger, seeing the development of our newspaper, but Xingyuan firmly refused, so Xie bore a grudge. (2) Xie Qing's behavior is despicable, and our colleagues are unwilling to associate with him. Huang Zhuangfei, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and Tang Mingzhi, the chief inspector, are corrupt and pervert the law, and our newspaper often exposes them, so they hate us to the bone. (3) Recently, as our newspaper has become more and more developed, we are preparing to expand, and they are deeply afraid that the Heluo Daily will be eclipsed, so they have devised a wicked plan to overthrow us. (4) Before the incident, because Xie Qing usually violated the law, various public organizations in the county accused him to the Provincial Party Department, and our newspaper's vice president, Zhao Ziyun, went to the province as a representative, which Xie Qing found out about, so he took his anger out on us. It is now heard that Xie Qing will be removed from his post because of this accusation. (5) Xingyuan is outspoken about Xie Qing, Huang Zhuangfei, and others' actions, so they have never been on good terms with Xingyuan.

Evidence Against the False Accusation of Being Reactionary: (1) Since our newspaper began publishing, it has sent twenty copies to the Central Party Department and fifteen copies to the National Government every day. For several months, the Central Party Department and the National Government have not made any criticisms of our newspaper's comments. (2) Xingyuan and Vice Presidents Guo Zibin and Zhao Ziyun, etc., have either been loyal to the Party and the State or have served their hometowns, and have never engaged in any reactionary activities. (3) If Xingyuan and others had engaged in reactionary activities, the local garrison would naturally have investigated and reported them at any time. Why does the garrison have no doubts about Xingyuan and others? (4) Xie Qing, Huang Zhuangfei, and others fabricated reactionary evidence. The day after the newspaper office was closed, County Magistrate Xie Suian had already stated that he did not recognize it. When the closure was carried out, the county magistrate asked if there was any reactionary evidence, and the Public Security Bureau reported that there was none. Moreover, the county magistrate reported to the province only that the Dazhonghua Daily had been sealed, without mentioning any "reactionary" words, which can be verified. (5) After our newspaper was sealed, local groups and elders of the entire county sent telegrams to the Pacification Commissioner's Office, the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, and the Department of Civil Affairs, guaranteeing that Xingyuan and others had not engaged in any reactionary activities. Summarizing the above two items of more than ten points, it is clear that Xie Qing and Huang Zhuangfei, etc., are maliciously accusing us and abusing their power for personal gain. Furthermore, in a central location of the capital, the closure of a newspaper should require an order from the highest authority. How could Xie Qing, a member of a county party department, be so arbitrary and act as he pleases? If he is not strictly investigated, a bad precedent will be set, and the future of our press will be in great danger. We hereby report this in detail, respectfully requesting that justice be upheld, that telegrams be sent to the Henan Provincial Party Department, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and the Provincial Government, to handle the matter impartially and order the lifting of the seal. We are immeasurably hopeful. Jia Xingyuan, President of the Luoyang Dazhonghua Daily; Zhao Ziyun, Vice President.

Temporary Alert in Nanshi and Zhabei Yesterday 138

Tranquility Returned in the Evening, Police Officers Withdrawn

The Municipal Public Security Bureau received a report yesterday that unemployed workers were about to take action. As a precaution, security was tightened yesterday, but there were no disturbances.

Temporary Alert: Wen Hongen, the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, received a report that, as a precaution, he specially notified the police stations in Nanshi Districts 1 and 2 and Zhabei Districts 4 and 5 to tighten security yesterday. After receiving the order, the district chiefs immediately increased the number of double posts on major roads.
